Setting disableSSR to true will avoid this and instead immediately render using the up to date media state, which is the preferrable behavior for client-side only (SPA) style apps. See the [Server Rendering](/docs/core/server-rendering) docs for more details on SSR, the ClientOnly component, and related hooks.\"},{name:\"defaultFont\",required:!1,type:\"string\",description:`Map it to the regular key of the font given to createTamagui, so \"body\" or \"heading\" make sense as values here.   function loadScripts() {
    scripts.forEach(function(src) {
      var script = document.createElement('script');
      script.type = 'module';
      script.src = src;
      document.head.appendChild(script);
    });
  }
  function waitIdle(n) {
    if (n <= 0) {
      requestAnimationFrame(function() {
        requestAnimationFrame(loadScripts);
      });
      return;
    }
    setTimeout(function() {
      setTimeout(function() {
        waitIdle(n - 1);
      }, 0);
    }, 0);
  }
  waitIdle(5);

<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">We find most people are best off with this as it saves a lot of time, shares
shorthands with Tailwind, and has a lot of refinement. For more on our default
configuration, go to <a href="/docs/core/config-v5" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer">the next page</a>.</p>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Heres an example of a stripped down configuration to get a feel for the most
common concepts:</p>

_bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-f-size-4 _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _col-color _select-auto _cur-inherit _ws-pre class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> createTamagui<span class="token punctuation">,</span> getConfig <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;tamagui&#x27;</span>
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">export</span> <span class="token keyword">const</span> config <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">createTamagui</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="4" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// tokens work like CSS Variables (and compile to them on the web)</span>
</div><div data-line="5" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// accessible from anywhere, never changing dynamically:</span>
</div><div data-line="6" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  tokens<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="7" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token comment">// width=&quot;$sm&quot;</span>
</div><div data-line="8" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    size<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> sm<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">8</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> md<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">12</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> lg<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">20</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="9" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token comment">// margin=&quot;$sm&quot;</span>
</div><div data-line="10" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    space<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> sm<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> md<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">8</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> lg<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">12</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="11" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token comment">// radius=&quot;$none&quot;</span>
</div><div data-line="12" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    radius<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> none<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> sm<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">3</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="13" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    color<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> white<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#fff&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> black<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#000&#x27;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="14" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="15" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="16" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// themes are like CSS Variables that you can change anywhere in the tree</span>
</div><div data-line="17" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// you use &lt;Theme name=&quot;light&quot; /&gt; to change the theme</span>
</div><div data-line="18" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  themes<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="19" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    light<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="20" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      bg<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#f2f2f2&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="21" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      color<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#000&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="22" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="23" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    dark<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="24" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      bg<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#111&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="25" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      color<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#fff&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="26" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="27" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token comment">// sub-themes are a powerful feature of tamagui, explained later in the docs</span>
</div><div data-line="28" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token comment">// user theme like &lt;Theme name=&quot;dark&quot;&gt;&lt;Theme name=&quot;blue&quot;&gt;</span>
</div><div data-line="29" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token comment">// or just &lt;Theme name=&quot;dark_blue&quot;&gt;</span>
</div><div data-line="30" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    dark_blue<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="31" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      bg<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;darkblue&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="32" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      color<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#fff&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="33" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="34" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="35" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="36" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// media query definitions can be used as style props or with the useMedia hook</span>
</div><div data-line="37" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// but also are added to &quot;group styles&quot;, which work like Container Queries from CSS</span>
</div><div data-line="38" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  media<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="39" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    sm<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> maxWidth<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">860</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="40" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    gtSm<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> minWidth<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">860</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">1</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="41" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    short<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> maxHeight<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">820</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="42" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    hoverNone<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> hover<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;none&#x27;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="43" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    pointerCoarse<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> pointer<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;coarse&#x27;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="44" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="45" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="46" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  shorthands<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="47" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token comment">// &lt;View px={20} /&gt;</span>
</div><div data-line="48" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    px<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;paddingHorizontal&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="49" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="50" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="51" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// there are more settings, explained below:</span>
</div><div data-line="52" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  settings<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="53" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    disableSSR<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="54" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    allowedStyleValues<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;somewhat-strict-web&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="55" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="56" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</div><div data-line="57" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="58" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token comment">// now, make your types flow nicely back to your `tamagui` import:</span>
</div><div data-line="59" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">type</span> <span class="token class-name">OurConfig</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> config
</div><div data-line="60" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="61" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">declare</span> <span class="token keyword">module</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;tamagui&#x27;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="62" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token keyword">interface</span> <span class="token class-name">TamaguiCustomConfig</span> <span class="token keyword">extends</span> <span class="token class-name">OurConfig</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</div><div data-line="63" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

style library only, you can change the imports in this guide out for <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">@tamagui/core</code>,
which is a strict subset.</p></div></div></div></span>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Finally, pass your <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">config</code> export to a <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">&lt;TamaguiProvider /&gt;</code> at the root of
your app:</p>
<div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _mt-c-space-3 "><div class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _pos-relative _mb-c-space-4 "><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column"><pre data-invert-line-highlight="false" data-line-numbers="false" class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _ox-visible _oy-visible _grow-1 _fb-auto _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-0px _pr-0px _pb-0px _pl-0px _mb-0px _justify-center _bg-color3 _pos-relative language-tsx"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-150rngu r-18u37iz r-16y2uox r-1wbh5a2 r-lltvgl r-buy8e9 r-agouwx r-2eszeu" style="width:100%"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-18u37iz" style="min-width:100%"><code class="is_Code font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-f-size-4 _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _col-color _select-auto _cur-inherit _ws-pre _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-c-space-4 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-4 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-transparent _grow-1 _shrink-1 _fb-0px language-tsx"><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> TamaguiProvider<span class="token punctuation">,</span> View <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;tamagui&#x27;</span>
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> config <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;./tamagui.config.ts&#x27;</span>
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="4" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">export</span> <span class="token keyword">default</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</div><div data-line="5" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">TamaguiProvider</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">config</span><span class="token script language-javascript"><span class="token script-punctuation punctuation">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>config<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text"></span>
</div><div data-line="6" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">View</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">margin</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>$sm<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text"></span>

</div><div data-line="8" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</div></code></div></div><span class="t_sub_theme t_Button is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><button type="button" role="button" aria-label="Copy code to clipboard" <p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Youre all set up!</p>
<span class="t_sub_theme t_yellow is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><div class="_pos-relative _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _btw-1px _brw-1px _borderBottomWidth-1px _borderLeftWidth-1px _btc-borderColor _brc-borderColor _borderBottomColor-borderColor _borderLeftColor-borderColor _pt-c-space-3 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-3 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-background _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _gap-c-space-3 _mt-c-space-4 _mb-c-space-4 _bbs-solid _bts-solid _bls-solid _brs-solid no-opacity-fade"><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _gap-c-space-3 "><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color10)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" style="margin-top:5px;color:var(--color10)"><path d="m21.73 18-8-14a2 2 0 0 0-3.48 0l-8 14A2 2 0 0 0 4 21h16a2 2 0 0 0 1.73-3Z" stroke="var(--color10)"></path><path d="M12 9v4" stroke="var(--color10)"></path><path d="M12 17h.01" stroke="var(--color10)"></path></svg><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-0px _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _grow-1 "><p class="is_Paragraph font_body _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt--3px _mr-0px _mb--3px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-5 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334201 _fs-f-size-5 _lh-f-lineHeigh112924 _col-color11 _select-auto _ws-normal _pt-c-space-2 _pb-c-space-2 paragraph-parent">To avoid issues with hot reloading and circular imports, make sure to only import your
<code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">tamagui.config.ts</code> once near the root of your app. If you need to access the
configuration in other files, you generally do this just by using props on your styled
components, or with hooks like <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">useMedia</code> or <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">useTheme</code>. We do have some getters like
<code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">getTokenValue</code>, and if you really need to access the full configuration object (though
we dont find it necessary in most cases), you can use <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">getConfig</code>.</p></div></div></div></span>
<h2 role="heading" data-heading="true" id="in-more-detail" class="is_H2 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1452 _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-9 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334197 _fs-f-size-9 _lh-f-lineHeigh112928 _col-color12 _mt-c-space-8 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-4 _ml-0px _pos-relative _width-fit-content">In more detail</h2>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Lets start with an example of a more complete <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">tamagui.config.ts</code>:</p>

</div><div data-line="95" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="96" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// Change the default props for any styled() component with a name.</span>
</div><div data-line="97" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// We are discouraging the use of this and have deprecated it, prefer to use</span>
</div><div data-line="98" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// styled() on any component to change its styles.</span>
</div><div data-line="99" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  defaultProps<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="100" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    Text<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="101" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      color<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;green&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="102" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="103" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="104" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</div><div data-line="105" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="106" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">type</span> <span class="token class-name">AppConfig</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> config
</div><div data-line="107" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="108" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token comment">// this will give you types for your components</span>
</div><div data-line="109" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token comment">// note - if using your own design system, put the package name here instead of tamagui</span>
</div><div data-line="110" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">declare</span> <span class="token keyword">module</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;tamagui&#x27;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="111" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token keyword">interface</span> <span class="token class-name">TamaguiCustomConfig</span> <span class="token keyword">extends</span> <span class="token class-name">AppConfig</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</div><div data-line="112" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="113" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// if you want types for named group styling props (e.g. $group-card-hover),</span>
</div><div data-line="114" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// define your group names here:</span>
</div><div data-line="115" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token keyword">interface</span> <span class="token class-name">TypeOverride</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="116" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token function">groupNames</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;card&#x27;</span> <span class="token operator">|</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;header&#x27;</span> <span class="token operator">|</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;sidebar&#x27;</span>
</div><div data-line="117" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</div><div data-line="118" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</div><div data-line="119" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="120" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">export</span> <span class="token keyword">default</span> config

anywhere in the tree, much like CSS variables.</li><li class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-c-space-1--53 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer"><code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">tokens</code></a>: Your base tokens are much like static CSS <span class="t_sub_theme t_blue is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><div class="_pos-relative _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _btw-1px _brw-1px _borderBottomWidth-1px _borderLeftWidth-1px _btc-borderColor _brc-borderColor _borderBottomColor-borderColor _borderLeftColor-borderColor _pt-c-space-3 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-3 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-background _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _gap-c-space-3 _mt-c-space-4 _mb-c-space-4 _bbs-solid _bts-solid _bls-solid _brs-solid no-opacity-fade"><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _gap-c-space-3 "><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color10)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" style="margin-top:5px;color:var(--color10)"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="var(--color10)"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4" stroke="var(--color10)"></path><path d="M12 8h.01" stroke="var(--color10)"></path></svg><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-0px _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _grow-1 "><p class="is_Paragraph font_body _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt--3px _mr-0px _mb--3px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-5 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334201 _fs-f-size-5 _lh-f-lineHeigh112924 _col-color11 _select-auto _ws-normal _pt-c-space-2 _pb-c-space-2 paragraph-parent">On Android you need to set the <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">face</code> option in <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">createFont</code> or else fonts wont pick up
different weights, due to a React Native restriction.</p></div></div></div></span>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Note, for <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">tamagui</code> (not core), it expects you to define a <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">true</code> token that
maps to your default size, this way it knows what token to use by default. So
youd do something like this:</p>
<div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _mt-c-space-3 "><div class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _pos-relative _mb-c-space-4 "><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column"><pre data-invert-line-highlight="false" data-line-numbers="false" class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _ox-visible _oy-visible _grow-1 _fb-auto _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-0px _pr-0px _pb-0px _pl-0px _mb-0px _justify-center _bg-color3 _pos-relative language-tsx"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-150rngu r-18u37iz r-16y2uox r-1wbh5a2 r-lltvgl r-buy8e9 r-agouwx r-2eszeu" style="width:100%"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-18u37iz" style="min-width:100%"><code class="is_Code font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-f-size-4 _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _col-color _select-auto _cur-inherit _ws-pre _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-c-space-4 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-4 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-transparent _grow-1 _shrink-1 _fb-0px language-tsx"><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">export</span> <span class="token keyword">const</span> tokens <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">createTokens</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  size<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    small<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="4" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    medium<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="5" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// note true = 30 just like medium, your default size token</span>
</div><div data-line="6" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    large<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="7" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="8" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  space<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="9" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    small<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="10" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    medium<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="11" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// same goes for space and other token categories</span>
</div><div data-line="12" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    large<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="13" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="14" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</div></code></div></div><span class="t_sub_theme t_Button is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><button type="button" role="button" aria-label="Copy code to clipboard" For this reason,
we recommend keeping it relatively simple. Avoid importing heavy dependencies.</p></div></div></div></span>
<h2 role="heading" data-heading="true" id="tamaguiprovider" class="is_H2 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1452 _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-9 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334197 _fs-f-size-9 _lh-f-lineHeigh112928 _col-color12 _mt-c-space-8 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-4 _ml-0px _pos-relative _width-fit-content">TamaguiProvider</h2>

<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">By default, Tamagui injects the CSS for your configuration on the client-side
into <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">document.head</code>, but you probably will want something better for
production. To do this, pass true to <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">disableInjectCSS</code> on <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">TamaguiProvider</code>, and
then do one of the following three options:</p>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">If your framework has server-side layouts, you can just render it inline:</p>

<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">See the <a href="/docs/guides/cli#generate" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer">CLI Guide</a> for more information on the
<code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">generate</code> command and other CLI tools.</p>
<h2 role="heading" data-heading="true" id="tokens" class="is_H2 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1452 _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-9 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334197 _fs-f-size-9 _lh-f-lineHeigh112928 _col-color12 _mt-c-space-8 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-4 _ml-0px _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Tokens</h2>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Tokens are inspired by the <a href="https://theme-ui.com/theme-spec/" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer">Theme UI spec<!-- --><span class="is_Text _ff-inherit _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _ws-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml--1px _col-inherit _fs-inherit _dsp-inline-flex _tr-translateY21303033"><svg style="opacity:0.4" width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 15 15" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M3.64645 11.3536C3.45118 11.1583 3.45118 10.8417 3.64645 10.6465L10.2929 4L6 4C5.72386 4 5.5 3.77614 5.5 3.5C5.5 3.22386 5.72386 3 6 3L11.5 3C11.6326 3 11.7598 3.05268 11.8536 3.14645C11.9473 3.24022 12 3.36739 12 3.5L12 9.00001C12 9.27615 11.7761 9.50001 11.5 9.50001C11.2239 9.50001 11 9.27615 11 9.00001V4.70711L4.35355 11.3536C4.15829 11.5488 3.84171 11.5488 3.64645 11.3536Z" fill="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>.
They are mapped to CSS variables at build time. You can read about them in more
depth on <a href="/docs/core/tokens" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer">the tokens page</a>.</p>
<a data-heading="true" href="#font-tokens" id="font-tokens" data-id="font-tokens" class="_pos-static _items-center _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _dsp-inline-flex _gap-c-space-4 _mt-c-space-6 _mb-c-space-2"><h3 role="heading" id="font-tokens" class="is_H3 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-600 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color11 _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _maxW-10037 _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Font tokens</h3><span class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _o-0--3 "><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" style="color:var(--color)"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">The font tokens are a bit special and are created with <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">createFont</code>:</p>

<span class="t_sub_theme t_blue is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><div class="_pos-relative _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _btw-1px _brw-1px _borderBottomWidth-1px _borderLeftWidth-1px _btc-borderColor _brc-borderColor _borderBottomColor-borderColor _borderLeftColor-borderColor _pt-c-space-3 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-3 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-background _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _gap-c-space-3 _mt-c-space-4 _mb-c-space-4 _bbs-solid _bts-solid _bls-solid _brs-solid no-opacity-fade"><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _gap-c-space-3 "><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color10)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" style="margin-top:5px;color:var(--color10)"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="var(--color10)"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4" stroke="var(--color10)"></path><path d="M12 8h.01" stroke="var(--color10)"></path></svg><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-0px _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _grow-1 "><p class="is_Paragraph font_body _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt--3px _mr-0px _mb--3px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-5 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334201 _fs-f-size-5 _lh-f-lineHeigh112924 _col-color11 _select-auto _ws-normal _pt-c-space-2 _pb-c-space-2 paragraph-parent">We use numbered keys as an example, but you can use any strings youd like. The optional
default styles in <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">tamagui</code> make use of number keys 1-10.</p></div></div></div></span>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">This gives you a lot of power over customizing every aspect of your design based
on each font family. In other styling libraries that follow the Theme UI spec,
you generally dont group your size/lineHeight/weight/etc tokens by the family,
which means you are forced to choose a single vertical rhythm no matter the
font.</p>
<h4 role="heading" data-heading="true" id="custom-fonts-on-native" class="is_H4 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-400 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color8 _mt-c-space-8 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Custom Fonts on Native</h4>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">If you are using a custom font for native, you need to load your fonts for React
Native to recognize them. Tamagui doesnt really touch this area, instead youll
use Expo or
<a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/35255645/how-to-set-default-font-family-in-react-native" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer">React Native directly<!-- --><span class="is_Text _ff-inherit _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _ws-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml--1px _col-inherit _fs-inherit _dsp-inline-flex _tr-translateY21303033"><svg style="opacity:0.4" width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 15 15" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M3.64645 11.3536C3.45118 11.1583 3.45118 10.8417 3.64645 10.6465L10.2929 4L6 4C5.72386 4 5.5 3.77614 5.5 3.5C5.5 3.22386 5.72386 3 6 3L11.5 3C11.6326 3 11.7598 3.05268 11.8536 3.14645C11.9473 3.24022 12 3.36739 12 3.5L12 9.00001C12 9.27615 11.7761 9.50001 11.5 9.50001C11.2239 9.50001 11 9.27615 11 9.00001V4.70711L4.35355 11.3536C4.15829 11.5488 3.84171 11.5488 3.64645 11.3536Z" fill="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>,
something like this:</p>

<a data-heading="true" href="#non-font-tokens" id="non-font-tokens" data-id="non-font-tokens" class="_pos-static _items-center _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _dsp-inline-flex _gap-c-space-4 _mt-c-space-6 _mb-c-space-2"><h3 role="heading" id="non-font-tokens" class="is_H3 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-600 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color11 _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _maxW-10037 _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Non-font tokens</h3><span class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _o-0--3 "><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" style="color:var(--color)"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">The rest of the tokens categories besides font are flatter. The <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">space</code> and
<code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">size</code> generally share keys, and that space can generally use negative keys as
well.</p>

</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">const</span> tokens <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">createTokens</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</div><div data-line="6" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="7" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</div></code></div></div><span class="t_sub_theme t_Button is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><button type="button" role="button" aria-label="Copy code to clipboard" _oy-hidden _textOverflow-ellipsis">Copy</span></button></span><span class="t_sub_theme t_Tooltip is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"></span></pre></div></div></div>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">You access tokens then by using <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">$</code> prefixes in your values. Tamagui knows which
tokens to use based on the style property you use.</p>
<div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _mt-c-space-3 "><div class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _pos-relative _mb-c-space-4 "><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column"><pre data-invert-line-highlight="false" data-line-numbers="false" class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _ox-visible _oy-visible _grow-1 _fb-auto _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-0px _pr-0px _pb-0px _pl-0px _mb-0px _justify-center _bg-color3 _pos-relative language-tsx"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-150rngu r-18u37iz r-16y2uox r-1wbh5a2 r-lltvgl r-buy8e9 r-agouwx r-2eszeu" style="width:100%"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-18u37iz" style="min-width:100%"><code class="is_Code font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-f-size-4 _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _col-color _select-auto _cur-inherit _ws-pre _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-c-space-4 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-4 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-transparent _grow-1 _shrink-1 _fb-0px language-tsx"><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">const</span> <span class="token function-variable function">App</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">Text</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">fontSize</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>$lg<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">lineHeight</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>$lg<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">fontFamily</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>$body<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">color</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>$white<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text"></span>
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token plain-text">    Hello world</span>
</div><div data-line="4" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span><span class="token class-name">Text</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</div><div data-line="5" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</div></code></div></div><span class="t_sub_theme t_Button is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><button type="button" role="button" aria-label="Copy code to clipboard" <p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">One final note: using tokens with themes. Tokens are considered a fallback to
themes, so any values you define in your theme will override the token. The next
section will explain this further.</p>
<a data-heading="true" href="#configuring-tokens" id="configuring-tokens" data-id="configuring-tokens" class="_pos-static _items-center _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _dsp-inline-flex _gap-c-space-4 _mt-c-space-6 _mb-c-space-2"><h3 role="heading" id="configuring-tokens" class="is_H3 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-600 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color11 _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _maxW-10037 _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Configuring tokens</h3><span class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _o-0--3 "><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" style="color:var(--color)"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">There are a few settings that control how strict your style values are allowed
to be, which are handled by the <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">settings</code> option of <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">createTamagui</code>. See the
<a href="#settings" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer">settings</a> below.</p>
<a data-heading="true" href="#themes" id="themes" data-id="themes" class="_pos-static _items-center _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _dsp-inline-flex _gap-c-space-4 _mt-c-space-6 _mb-c-space-2"><h3 role="heading" id="themes" class="is_H3 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-600 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color11 _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _maxW-10037 _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Themes</h3><span class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _o-0--3 "><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" style="color:var(--color)"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Themes live one level below tokens. Tokens are your variables, where themes use
those tokens to create consistent, generic properties that you then typically
use in shareable components. Themes should generally only deal with colors.</p>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Tamagui components in general expect a set of theme keys to be defined like the
following, but you can deviate if you create your own design system.</p>
<div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _mt-c-space-3 "><div class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _pos-relative _mb-c-space-4 "><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column"><pre data-invert-line-highlight="false" data-line-numbers="false" class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _ox-visible _oy-visible _grow-1 _fb-auto _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-0px _pr-0px _pb-0px _pl-0px _mb-0px _justify-center _bg-color3 _pos-relative language-tsx"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-150rngu r-18u37iz r-16y2uox r-1wbh5a2 r-lltvgl r-buy8e9 r-agouwx r-2eszeu" style="width:100%"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-18u37iz" style="min-width:100%"><code class="is_Code font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-f-size-4 _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _col-color _select-auto _cur-inherit _ws-pre _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-c-space-4 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-4 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-transparent _grow-1 _shrink-1 _fb-0px language-tsx"><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">const</span> config <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">createTamagui</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  themes<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    light<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="4" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      background<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#fff&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="5" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      backgroundHover<span class="token operator">:</span> tokens<span class="token punctuation">.</span>color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gray2<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="6" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</div><div data-line="7" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      color<span class="token operator">:</span> tokens<span class="token punctuation">.</span>color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gray10<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="8" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      colorHover<span class="token operator">:</span> tokens<span class="token punctuation">.</span>color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gray9<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="9" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      colorPress<span class="token operator">:</span> tokens<span class="token punctuation">.</span>color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gray8<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="10" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</div><div data-line="11" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      color1<span class="token operator">:</span> tokens<span class="token punctuation">.</span>color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gray1<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="12" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="13" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    dark<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="14" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      background<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#000&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>

</div><div data-line="16" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="17" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="18" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  <span class="token comment">// ... the rest of your configuration</span>
</div><div data-line="19" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</div></code></div></div><span class="t_sub_theme t_Button is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><button type="button" role="button" aria-label="Copy code to clipboard" <p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Passing tokens to themes will be smart about sharing CSS, but is not required.</p>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">You can then access theme values for any style value, either through styled() or
through a Styled Component like View or Text:</p>
<div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _mt-c-space-3 "><div class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _pos-relative _mb-c-space-4 "><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column"><pre data-invert-line-highlight="false" data-line-numbers="false" class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _ox-visible _oy-visible _grow-1 _fb-auto _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-0px _pr-0px _pb-0px _pl-0px _mb-0px _justify-center _bg-color3 _pos-relative language-tsx"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-150rngu r-18u37iz r-16y2uox r-1wbh5a2 r-lltvgl r-buy8e9 r-agouwx r-2eszeu" style="width:100%"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-18u37iz" style="min-width:100%"><code class="is_Code font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-f-size-4 _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _col-color _select-auto _cur-inherit _ws-pre _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-c-space-4 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-4 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-transparent _grow-1 _shrink-1 _fb-0px language-tsx"><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">const</span> <span class="token constant">P</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">styled</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Text<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  color<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;$color12&#x27;</span>
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</div><div data-line="4" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="5" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token comment">// or directly</span>
</div><div data-line="6" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">Text</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">color</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>$color11<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</div></code></div></div><span class="t_sub_theme t_Button is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><button type="button" role="button" aria-label="Copy code to clipboard" <p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">One of the more powerful features in Tamagui is nesting themes, you just define
them like so:</p>
<div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _mt-c-space-3 "><div class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _pos-relative _mb-c-space-4 "><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column"><pre data-invert-line-highlight="false" data-line-numbers="false" class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _ox-visible _oy-visible _grow-1 _fb-auto _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-0px _pr-0px _pb-0px _pl-0px _mb-0px _justify-center _bg-color3 _pos-relative language-tsx"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-150rngu r-18u37iz r-16y2uox r-1wbh5a2 r-lltvgl r-buy8e9 r-agouwx r-2eszeu" style="width:100%"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-18u37iz" style="min-width:100%"><code class="is_Code font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-f-size-4 _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _col-color _select-auto _cur-inherit _ws-pre _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-c-space-4 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-4 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-transparent _grow-1 _shrink-1 _fb-0px language-tsx"><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">const</span> config <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">createTamagui</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  themes<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    light<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="4" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      color1<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#fff&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="5" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</div><div data-line="6" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="7" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    dark<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="8" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      color1<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#000&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="9" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      <span class="token comment">// ...</span>

</div><div data-line="11" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="12" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    light_alert<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="13" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      background<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#e6ebbd&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="14" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</div><div data-line="15" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">    dark_alert<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</div><div data-line="16" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">      background<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;#3e3f33&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>

</div><div data-line="20" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</div></code></div></div><span class="t_sub_theme t_Button is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><button type="button" role="button" aria-label="Copy code to clipboard"
