<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Themes work just like CSS variables, they can be changed anywhere in the tree.
Sub-themes can be subsets of parent themes likewise as their values will fall
back to the parent theme. They can also be nested as deeply as you like - so
even <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">light_alert_subtle</code> is possible.</p>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">For more on themes, see the <a href="/docs/core/themes" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer">themes docs</a>, and more
<a href="/docs/guides/theme-builder" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer">advanced theme building library</a>.</p>
<a data-heading="true" href="#media" id="media" data-id="media" class="_pos-static _items-center _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _dsp-inline-flex _gap-c-space-4 _mt-c-space-6 _mb-c-space-2"><h3 role="heading" id="media" class="is_H3 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-600 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color11 _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _maxW-10037 _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Media</h3><span class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _o-0--3 "><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" style="color:var(--color)"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">For more full docs on media queries, see the
<a href="/docs/core/use-media" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer">useMedia docs page</a>.</p>
<a data-heading="true" href="#animations" id="animations" data-id="animations" class="_pos-static _items-center _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _dsp-inline-flex _gap-c-space-4 _mt-c-space-6 _mb-c-space-2"><h3 role="heading" id="animations" class="is_H3 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-600 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color11 _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _maxW-10037 _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Animations</h3><span class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _o-0--3 "><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" style="color:var(--color)"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">Tamagui supports four animation drivers that can be swapped out per-platform:</p>
<ul class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _ml-c-space-4 _mr-c-space-2 _mt-c-space-4 _mb-c-space-4"><li class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-c-space-1--53 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-list-item _pb-c-space-1 docs-paragraph" style="list-style-type:disc"><a href="/docs/core/animations-css" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer"><code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">@tamagui/animations-css</code></a> - CSS transition based
animations (lightest)</li><li class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-c-space-1--53 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-list-item _pb-c-space-1 docs-paragraph" style="list-style-type:disc"><a href="/docs/core/animations-react-native" role="link" class="is_Paragraph font_body _outlineColor-0focus-visible-outlineColo114 _outlineWidth-0focus-visible-2px _outlineStyle-0focus-visible-solid _outlineOffset-0focus-visible-2px _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-inline _cur-pointer"><code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">@tamagui/animations-react-native</code></a> -

_o-0--65">For SSR compatibility on the web, Tamagui will render once with the settings from mediaQueryDefaultActive set for all media queries. Then, it will render again after the initial render using the proper media query values. This is so that the hydrating components will match the server. Setting disableSSR to true will avoid this and instead immediately render using the up to date media state, which is the preferrable behavior for client-side only (SPA) style apps. See the [Server Rendering](/docs/core/server-rendering) docs for more details on SSR, the ClientOnly component, and related hooks.</p></div></div><div class="is_Separator _dsp-flex _items-stretch _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-3 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334203 _fs-f-size-3 _lh-f-lineHeigh112922 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _o-0--65">Only for web, when using group styles Tamagui uses container queries. When using a group on a containing element, Tamagui defaults to setting &quot;container-type&quot; in CSS to &quot;inline-size&quot;.</p></div></div><div class="is_Separator _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fd-column _fb-0px _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _btc-backgroundF3405682 _brc-backgroundF3405682 _borderBottomColor-backgroundF3405682 _borderLeftColor-backgroundF3405682 _btw-0px _brw-0px _borderBottomWidth-1px _borderLeftWidth-0px _grow-1 _height-0px _maxH-0px _bbs-solid _bts-solid _bls-solid _brs-solid _mt-2px _mb-2px _tr-translateY-1736186894 "></div></li></div>
<h4 role="heading" data-heading="true" id="type-strictness" class="is_H4 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-400 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color8 _mt-c-space-8 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Type strictness</h4>
<h4 role="heading" data-heading="true" id="allowedstylevalues" class="is_H4 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-400 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color8 _mt-c-space-8 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _pos-relative _width-fit-content"><code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">allowedStyleValues</code></h4>
<ul class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _ml-c-space-4 _mr-c-space-2 _mt-c-space-4 _mb-c-space-4"><li class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-c-space-1--53 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-list-item _pb-c-space-1 docs-paragraph" style="list-style-type:disc"><code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">false (default)</code>: allows any string (or number for styles that accept
numbers)</li><li class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-c-space-1--53 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-list-item _pb-c-space-1 docs-paragraph" style="list-style-type:disc"><code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">strict</code>: only allows tokens for any token-enabled properties</li><li class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-c-space-1--53 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-list-item _pb-c-space-1 docs-paragraph" style="list-style-type:disc"><code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">strict-web</code>: same as strict but allows for web-specific tokens like
auto/inherit</li><li class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-c-space-1--53 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-list-item _pb-c-space-1 docs-paragraph" style="list-style-type:disc"><code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">somewhat-strict</code>: allow tokens or:<!-- -->
<ul class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _ml-c-space-4 _mr-c-space-2 _mt-c-space-4 _mb-c-space-4"><li class="is_Paragraph _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">space/size</code>: string% or numbers</li><li class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-c-space-1--53 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 </li><li class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-c-space-1--53 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-list-item _pb-c-space-1 docs-paragraph" style="list-style-type:disc"><code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">somewhat-strict-web</code>: same as somewhat-strict but allows for web-specific
tokens</li></ul>
<div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _mt-c-space-3 "><div class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _pos-relative _mb-c-space-4 "><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column"><pre data-invert-line-highlight="false" data-line-numbers="false" class="_dsp-flex _items-stretch _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _ox-visible _oy-visible _grow-1 _fb-auto _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-0px _pr-0px _pb-0px _pl-0px _mb-0px _justify-center _bg-color3 _pos-relative language-tsx"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-150rngu r-18u37iz r-16y2uox r-1wbh5a2 r-lltvgl r-buy8e9 r-agouwx r-2eszeu" style="width:100%"><div class="css-g5y9jx r-18u37iz" style="min-width:100%"><code class="is_Code font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-4 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-f-size-4 _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _col-color _select-auto _cur-inherit _ws-pre _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _pt-c-space-4 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-4 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-transparent _grow-1 _shrink-1 _fb-0px language-tsx"><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">type</span> <span class="token class-name">AllowedValueSetting</span> <span class="token operator">=</span>

<h4 role="heading" data-heading="true" id="autocompletespecifictokens" class="is_H4 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-400 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color8 _mt-c-space-8 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _pos-relative _width-fit-content"><code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">autocompleteSpecificTokens</code></h4>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">The VSCode autocomplete puts specific tokens above the regular ones, which leads
to worse DX. If true this setting removes the specific token from types for the
defined categories.</p>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">If set to <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">except-special</code>, specific tokens will autocomplete only if they dont
normally use one of the special token groups: space, size, radius, zIndex,
color.</p>
<a data-heading="true" href="#environment-settings" id="environment-settings" data-id="environment-settings" class="_pos-static _items-center _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _dsp-inline-flex _gap-c-space-4 _mt-c-space-6 _mb-c-space-2"><h3 role="heading" id="environment-settings" class="is_H3 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-600 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color11 _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _maxW-10037 _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Environment Settings</h3><span class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _o-0--3 "><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" style="color:var(--color)"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">A few things in Tamagui can be configured via environment variables. Doing it
this way lets us avoid extra code being shipped to the client, as your
bundler can tree shake the unused code easily when using environment variables.
You should be sure to either use the Vite or Webpack Tamagui plugins, or
configure your bundler to define the environment variables for tree shaking. On
native, it is not a concern as the extra size is minimal.</p>
<a data-heading="true" href="#tree-shaking-themes" id="tree-shaking-themes" data-id="tree-shaking-themes" class="_pos-static _items-center _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _dsp-inline-flex _gap-c-space-4 _mt-c-space-6 _mb-c-space-2"><h3 role="heading" id="tree-shaking-themes" class="is_H3 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-600 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color11 _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _maxW-10037 _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Tree Shaking Themes</h3><span class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _o-0--3 "><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" style="color:var(--color)"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph"><strong class="is_Paragraph font_body _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _col-color _fw-700 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334202 _fs-inherit _lh-f-lineHeigh112923 _select-auto _ws-normal">Production Optimization</strong> - Theme JS can grow to 20KB or more. Since Tamagui can hydrate themes from CSS variables, you can remove the themes JS from your client bundle for better Lighthouse scores.</p>
<p class="is_Paragraph font_body _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt-c-space-2 _mr-0px _mb-c-space-2 _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-6 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334200 _fs-f-size-6 _lh-f-lineHeigh112925 _col-color _select-auto _ws-normal _dsp-block docs-paragraph">This works because Tamagui generates CSS variables for all theme values. On the
client, it reads these from the DOM instead of needing the JS object.</p>
<span class="t_sub_theme t_yellow is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><div class="_pos-relative _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _btw-1px _brw-1px _borderBottomWidth-1px _borderLeftWidth-1px _btc-borderColor _brc-borderColor _borderBottomColor-borderColor _borderLeftColor-borderColor _pt-c-space-3 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-3 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-background _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _gap-c-space-3 _mt-c-space-4 _mb-c-space-4 _bbs-solid _bts-solid _bls-solid _brs-solid no-opacity-fade"><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _gap-c-space-3 "><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color10)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" style="margin-top:5px;color:var(--color10)"><path d="m21.73 18-8-14a2 2 0 0 0-3.48 0l-8 14A2 2 0 0 0 4 21h16a2 2 0 0 0 1.73-3Z" stroke="var(--color10)"></path><path d="M12 9v4" stroke="var(--color10)"></path><path d="M12 17h.01" stroke="var(--color10)"></path></svg><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-0px _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _grow-1 "><p class="is_Paragraph font_body _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt--3px _mr-0px _mb--3px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-5 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334201 _fs-f-size-5 _lh-f-lineHeigh112924 _col-color11 _select-auto _ws-normal _pt-c-space-2 _pb-c-space-2 paragraph-parent">This optimization only applies to SSR web apps (Next.js, One, Vite SSR). It doesnt
apply to Metro/Expo or static sites. Note that v5 themes are already more optimized than
v4, so this is mainly relevant if chasing the last few Lighthouse points.</p></div></div></div></span>
<a data-heading="true" href="#setup" id="setup" data-id="setup" class="_pos-static _items-center _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _dsp-inline-flex _gap-c-space-4 _mt-c-space-6 _mb-c-space-2"><h3 role="heading" id="setup" class="is_H3 font_heading _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _select-auto _ws-normal _tt-f-transform1451 _ff-f-family _fw-600 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334198 _fs-f-size-8 _lh-f-lineHeigh112927 _col-color11 _mt-0px _mr-0px _mb-0px _ml-0px _maxW-10037 _pos-relative _width-fit-content">Setup</h3><span class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _o-0--3 "><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" style="color:var(--color)"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71" stroke="var(--color)"></path></svg></span></a>

<span class="t_sub_theme t_green is_Theme" style="color:var(--color);display:contents"><div class="_pos-relative _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-column _btw-1px _brw-1px _borderBottomWidth-1px _borderLeftWidth-1px _btc-borderColor _brc-borderColor _borderBottomColor-borderColor _borderLeftColor-borderColor _pt-c-space-3 _pr-c-space-4 _pb-c-space-3 _pl-c-space-4 _bg-background _btlr-c-radius-4 _btrr-c-radius-4 _bbrr-c-radius-4 _bblr-c-radius-4 _gap-c-space-3 _mt-c-space-4 _mb-c-space-4 _bbs-solid _bts-solid _bls-solid _brs-solid no-opacity-fade"><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-0 _fd-row _gap-c-space-3 "><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--color10)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" style="margin-top:5px;color:var(--color10)"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14" stroke="var(--color10)"></path><path d="m9 11 3 3L22 4" stroke="var(--color10)"></path></svg><div class="_pos-static _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-0px _bxs-border-box _minH-0px _minW-0px _shrink-1 _fd-column _grow-1 "><p class="is_Paragraph font_body _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-break-word _mt--3px _mr-0px _mb--3px _ml-0px _ff-f-family _fw-f-weight-5 _ls-f-letterSpa1360334201 _fs-f-size-5 _lh-f-lineHeigh112924 _col-color11 _select-auto _ws-normal _pt-c-space-2 _pb-c-space-2 paragraph-parent">This optimization requires server-side rendering. The CSS must be rendered on the server
for the client to hydrate from it. Make sure youre using <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit _btlr-c-radius-3 _btrr-c-radius-3 _bbrr-c-radius-3 _bblr-c-radius-3 _fs-9037 _lh-7037 _pr-0--637 _pl-0--637 _pt-0--4537 _pb-0--4537 _ws-pre">config.getCSS()</code> or the
bundler plugins <code class="is_CodeInline font_mono _dsp-inline _bxs-border-box _ww-inherit _mt-0px _mr--0--137 _mb-0px _ml--0--137 _ff-f-family _col-color12 _select-auto _bg-color3 _cur-inherit option.</p></div></div></div></span></span></span></div><div class="_maxW-_gtSm_760px _maxW-_gtMd_810px _maxW-_gtLg_810px _pos-relative _dsp-flex _items-stretch _fb-auto _bxs-border-box _minH-0px
